## Measurement Paths

| Track | Canonical path | Update rule |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Measurement register and anti-churn update map | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-measurement-register.md` | Read first when updating percentages, map paths, latest backup pointers, state batons, or wave evidence paths. |
| Function-quality closure and `0 / 0 / 0` debt | `subagents/ghidra-static-reaudit/queue/current/static-reaudit-queue.json` | Refresh from live Ghidra queue exports before claiming a function-count change. |
| Current-risk continuity denominator and focused candidate source | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-current-risk-ledger.json`; `subagents/ghidra-static-reaudit/wave1108-current-risk-rank/wave1108-current-focused-candidates.tsv` | The generated ledger enforces the `1179` continuity denominator; the TSV is the live focused-candidate artifact, currently `1117`, and must not be used alone as the active denominator. |
| Active percentage and latest wave baton | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-progress.json` | Update every completed static wave; mirror to `lore-book/reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-progress.json`. |
| Unique-address accounting | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-current-risk-ledger.json` | Regenerate with `py -3 tools/static_reaudit_accounting_guard.py --write-ledger`; do not hand-edit counts. |
| Human system map | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/mapped-systems.md` | Keep this top anchor and table current so system-map readers see the same measured state as the JSON ledger. |
| Accounting guard and done definition | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/static-reaudit-accounting-guard.md` | Update when the active denominator, latest wave, or static completion definition changes. |
| Wave evidence packet | `reverse-engineering/binary-analysis/wave1219-final-score16-current-risk-review.md` and `release/readiness/wave1219_final_score16_current_risk_review_2026-06-07.md` | One focused note plus one public-safe readiness note per completed Ghidra wave. |
| Ghidra backup verification | `subagents/ghidra-static-reaudit/wave1219-final-score16-current-risk-review/backup-summary.json` | Private ignored evidence; public docs record only path/counts/hash-diff summary. |
| Probe enforcement | `tools/wave1219_final_score16_current_risk_review.py`, `tools/static_reaudit_accounting_guard.py`, and `tools/static_reaudit_final_closeout_wave1220.py` | Probes must fail on stale percentages, stale backup paths, missing docs/mirrors, unresolved current-count drift, or overclaims. |

## Static Done Definition

Static binary RE is done when every active static lane for the loaded Steam retail Ghidra database is closed: no unreviewed active static-risk rows remain, no known static-lane evidence gap remains, and subsystem contracts are closed for static purposes with implementation-facing maps, source-parity hypotheses, exact-layout unknowns, patch anchors, and rebuild-risk boundaries explicitly recorded. The active pre-runtime gate is `1179/1179 current-risk focused rows reviewed or superseded with bounded static evidence`, while preserving `6411/6411` function-quality closure with `0 / 0 / 0` static debt and `1560/1560` expanded post-100 static surface closure. No active static lane is skipped, waived, or deferred merely because it is hard; remaining unknowns must be explicitly outside static-only proof.

This definition deliberately excludes runtime gameplay behavior, visual QA, exact concrete runtime layouts unless separately proven, exact source-body identity, BEA patching behavior, and rebuild parity. Wave911 is historical-retired/non-reconstructable provenance, not the active completion gate. A single subsystem can move to runtime proof earlier only when its own static contract and patch/static anchors are closed; that is scoped proof, not global static completion.

For clean-room usefulness, each major subsystem contract must separate retail static proof, source-parity hypotheses, exact-layout unknowns, runtime-test targets, patch-byte assumptions, and rebuild-parity claims. Final static closeout requires a fresh queue/risk refresh showing no unreviewed active focused rows at the current threshold and passing the static accounting/docs/probe gates. No active static lane is skipped, waived, or deferred merely because it is hard; remaining unknowns must be explicitly outside static-only proof.

Use these as static Ghidra/export-contract metrics, not runtime or rebuild certification:

## How To Use This Map

- Treat this file as the human system map that points to canonical evidence, not as the machine counter. The counters live in `static-reaudit-progress.json`.
- Treat `100.00%` static closure as "every loaded Ghidra function object has bounded name/signature/comment-quality treatment, the expanded post-100 audit surface has been reviewed, and the Wave1108 current-risk denominator is closed at `1179/1179`." This is static pre-runtime closeout, not runtime or rebuild certification.
- Keep proof domains separate: static coherence, source parity, exact layout, runtime behavior, BEA patching, and rebuild parity are different claims.
- Before runtime/visual/product work, use this map plus the readiness notes to turn scattered function proof into subsystem contracts and layout hypotheses.

## Static Closeout Acceptance

- Keep using Ghidra/readiness evidence as authority; do not promote stale scratch candidate rows without fresh export checks.
- Wave911 focused remains historical-retired/non-reconstructable at `812/1408 = 57.67%`; do not convert it back into the active denominator.
- Current static closeout gate: function-quality closure `6411/6411 = 100.00%`, static debt `0 / 0 / 0`, expanded post-100 surface `1560/1560 = 100.00%`, current-risk focused closure `1179/1179 = 100.00%`, and remaining active focused work: 0.
- Wave1220 static closeout acceptance: active current-risk focused accounting is `1179/1179 = 100.00%`; remaining active focused work: 0; system contracts are the implementation-facing static map for clean-room planning.
- For clean-room rebuild planning, separate source-parity hypotheses from concrete retail layouts and from runtime behavior.
- Leave runtime proof, visual QA, WinUI feature work, BEA patch behavior, and rebuild parity until the specific static contract slice being tested is selected and its runtime/proof plan is explicit.
